case = {'description': 'Tests that when a service_catalog is provided, the LLM uses the canonical service name instead of sho...15.0}]}, 'tool_called': 'AddJobTool'}, 'feature_spec': '004-line-items', 'id': 'spec-004-line-item-catalog-match', ...}

    @pytest.mark.llm_validation
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    @pytest.mark.parametrize("case", test_cases, ids=lambda c: c["id"])
    async def test_llm_parsing(case):
        """
        Parametric test for LLM parsing logic.
        Runs against the real LLM (OpenRouter/Gemini).
    
        Each test case can include:
        - user_input: The raw user message
        - user_context: Role, settings, and other context passed to the LLM
        - service_catalog: Optional catalog of services for line item matching
        - system_time: Optional ISO timestamp for time-relative queries
        - expected_logic: Expected tool call and/or response substrings
        """
        user_input = case["user_input"]
        expected_logic = case.get("expected_logic", {})
        user_context = case.get("user_context", {})
        service_catalog = case.get("service_catalog")
        system_time = case.get("system_time")
    
        # Extract channel from user_context (defaults to WHATSAPP for backward compat)
        channel_name = user_context.pop("channel", "WHATSAPP") if "channel" in user_context else "WHATSAPP"
    
        parser = LLMParser()
    
        # Execute parsing with all context variables
        result = await parser.parse(
            user_input,
            system_time=system_time,
            service_catalog=service_catalog,
            channel_name=channel_name,
            user_context=user_context
        )
    
        expected_tool = expected_logic.get("tool_called")
        expected_args = expected_logic.get("expected_args", {})
        required_substring = expected_logic.get("required_response_substring")
    
        if expected_tool:
            assert result is not None, f"Expected tool {expected_tool}, but got None"
            actual_tool = result.__class__.__name__
            assert actual_tool == expected_tool, f"Tool mismatch. Expected {expected_tool}, got {actual_tool}"
    
            # Verify arguments
            actual_args = result.dict(exclude_none=True)
            for key, val in expected_args.items():
                assert key in actual_args, f"Missing expected argument '{key}' in {actual_tool}"
    
                # Special handling for floats/rounding
                if isinstance(val, float) and isinstance(actual_args[key], float):
                    assert pytest.approx(actual_args[key]) == val, f"Argument '{key}' mismatch. Expected {val}, got {actual_args[key]}"
                # Special handling for line_items (list of dicts)
                elif key == "line_items" and isinstance(val, list):
>                   _verify_line_items(val, actual_args[key])

    def _verify_line_items(expected_items: list, actual_items: list):
        """
        Verify that line items match expected values.
        Uses partial matching: only checks fields specified in expected.
        """
        assert len(actual_items) >= len(expected_items), \
            f"Expected at least {len(expected_items)} line items, got {len(actual_items)}"
    
        for i, expected_item in enumerate(expected_items):
            actual_item = actual_items[i] if i < len(actual_items) else {}

case = {'description': "Validates that with a catalog, the LLM does NOT shorten 'Exterior Window Cleaning' to 'windows'.", 'e...ce': 60.0}, 'tool_called': 'AddJobTool'}, 'feature_spec': '004-line-items', 'id': 'spec-004-line-item-no-shorten', ...}

    @pytest.mark.llm_validation
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    @pytest.mark.parametrize("case", test_cases, ids=lambda c: c["id"])
    async def test_llm_parsing(case):
        """
        Parametric test for LLM parsing logic.
        Runs against the real LLM (OpenRouter/Gemini).
    
        Each test case can include:
        - user_input: The raw user message
        - user_context: Role, settings, and other context passed to the LLM
        - service_catalog: Optional catalog of services for line item matching
        - system_time: Optional ISO timestamp for time-relative queries
        - expected_logic: Expected tool call and/or response substrings
        """
        user_input = case["user_input"]
        expected_logic = case.get("expected_logic", {})
        user_context = case.get("user_context", {})
        service_catalog = case.get("service_catalog")
        system_time = case.get("system_time")
    
        # Extract channel from user_context (defaults to WHATSAPP for backward compat)
        channel_name = user_context.pop("channel", "WHATSAPP") if "channel" in user_context else "WHATSAPP"
    
        parser = LLMParser()
    
        # Execute parsing with all context variables
        result = await parser.parse(
            user_input,
            system_time=system_time,
            service_catalog=service_catalog,
            channel_name=channel_name,
            user_context=user_context
        )
    
        expected_tool = expected_logic.get("tool_called")
        expected_args = expected_logic.get("expected_args", {})
        required_substring = expected_logic.get("required_response_substring")
    
        if expected_tool:
            assert result is not None, f"Expected tool {expected_tool}, but got None"
            actual_tool = result.__class__.__name__

CREATE TABLE businesses (
	id INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	name VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	payment_link VARCHAR, 
	created_at DATETIME NOT NULL, 
	stripe_customer_id VARCHAR, 
	stripe_subscription_id VARCHAR, 
	subscription_status VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	seat_limit INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	active_addons JSON NOT NULL, 
	quickbooks_connected BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	quickbooks_last_sync DATETIME, 
	clerk_org_id VARCHAR, 
	workflow_invoicing VARCHAR, 
	workflow_quoting VARCHAR, 
	workflow_payment_timing VARCHAR, 
	workflow_tax_inclusive BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_include_payment_terms BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_enable_reminders BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_show_whatsapp_button BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_pipeline_quoted_stage BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_job_creation_default VARCHAR, 
	workflow_distance_unit VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	workflow_auto_quote_followup BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_quote_followup_delay_hrs INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	workflow_auto_review_requests BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_review_request_delay_hrs INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	workflow_review_link VARCHAR, 
	marketing_settings JSON NOT NULL, 
	default_city VARCHAR, 
	default_country VARCHAR, 
	default_tax_rate FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	invite_code VARCHAR(20), 
	message_count_current_period INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	billing_cycle_anchor DATETIME, 
	message_credits INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	PRIMARY KEY (id), 
	UNIQUE (clerk_org_id)
)

case = {'description': "Tests math calculation: when user says '12 windows for $60', total is $60, unit price is $5", 'expect...5.0}], 'price': 60.0}, 'tool_called': 'AddJobTool'}, 'feature_spec': '004-line-items', 'id': 'spec-004-math-test', ...}

    @pytest.mark.llm_validation
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    @pytest.mark.parametrize("case", test_cases, ids=lambda c: c["id"])
    async def test_llm_parsing(case):
        """
        Parametric test for LLM parsing logic.
        Runs against the real LLM (OpenRouter/Gemini).
    
        Each test case can include:
        - user_input: The raw user message
        - user_context: Role, settings, and other context passed to the LLM
        - service_catalog: Optional catalog of services for line item matching
        - system_time: Optional ISO timestamp for time-relative queries
        - expected_logic: Expected tool call and/or response substrings
        """
        user_input = case["user_input"]
        expected_logic = case.get("expected_logic", {})
        user_context = case.get("user_context", {})
        service_catalog = case.get("service_catalog")
        system_time = case.get("system_time")
    
        # Extract channel from user_context (defaults to WHATSAPP for backward compat)
        channel_name = user_context.pop("channel", "WHATSAPP") if "channel" in user_context else "WHATSAPP"
    
        parser = LLMParser()
    
        # Execute parsing with all context variables
        result = await parser.parse(
            user_input,
            system_time=system_time,
            service_catalog=service_catalog,
            channel_name=channel_name,
            user_context=user_context
        )
    
        expected_tool = expected_logic.get("tool_called")
        expected_args = expected_logic.get("expected_args", {})
        required_substring = expected_logic.get("required_response_substring")
    
        if expected_tool:
            assert result is not None, f"Expected tool {expected_tool}, but got None"
            actual_tool = result.__class__.__name__
            assert actual_tool == expected_tool, f"Tool mismatch. Expected {expected_tool}, got {actual_tool}"
    
            # Verify arguments
            actual_args = result.dict(exclude_none=True)
            for key, val in expected_args.items():
                assert key in actual_args, f"Missing expected argument '{key}' in {actual_tool}"
    
                # Special handling for floats/rounding
                if isinstance(val, float) and isinstance(actual_args[key], float):
                    assert pytest.approx(actual_args[key]) == val, f"Argument '{key}' mismatch. Expected {val}, got {actual_args[key]}"
                # Special handling for line_items (list of dicts)
                elif key == "line_items" and isinstance(val, list):
>                   _verify_line_items(val, actual_args[key])

    def _verify_line_items(expected_items: list, actual_items: list):
        """
        Verify that line items match expected values.
        Uses partial matching: only checks fields specified in expected.
        """
        assert len(actual_items) >= len(expected_items), \
            f"Expected at least {len(expected_items)} line items, got {len(actual_items)}"
    
        for i, expected_item in enumerate(expected_items):
            actual_item = actual_items[i] if i < len(actual_items) else {}
    
            for field, expected_val in expected_item.items():
                assert field in actual_item, \
                    f"Line item {i}: Missing field '{field}'. Actual: {actual_item}"
    
                actual_val = actual_item[field]
    
                # Description matching: case-insensitive contains check for flexibility
                if field == "description":

CREATE TABLE businesses (
	id INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	name VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	payment_link VARCHAR, 
	created_at DATETIME NOT NULL, 
	stripe_customer_id VARCHAR, 
	stripe_subscription_id VARCHAR,

	seat_limit INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	active_addons JSON NOT NULL, 
	quickbooks_connected BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	quickbooks_last_sync DATETIME, 
	clerk_org_id VARCHAR, 
	workflow_invoicing VARCHAR, 
	workflow_quoting VARCHAR, 
	workflow_payment_timing VARCHAR, 
	workflow_tax_inclusive BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_include_payment_terms BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_enable_reminders BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_show_whatsapp_button BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_pipeline_quoted_stage BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_job_creation_default VARCHAR, 
	workflow_distance_unit VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	workflow_auto_quote_followup BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_quote_followup_delay_hrs INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	workflow_auto_review_requests BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_review_request_delay_hrs INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	workflow_review_link VARCHAR, 
	marketing_settings JSON NOT NULL, 
	default_city VARCHAR, 
	default_country VARCHAR, 
	default_tax_rate FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	invite_code VARCHAR(20), 
	message_count_current_period INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	billing_cycle_anchor DATETIME, 
	message_credits INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	PRIMARY KEY (id), 
	UNIQUE (clerk_org_id)
)

    @pytest.mark.llm_validation
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    @pytest.mark.parametrize("case", test_cases, ids=lambda c: c["id"])
    async def test_llm_parsing(case):
        """
        Parametric test for LLM parsing logic.
        Runs against the real LLM (OpenRouter/Gemini).
    
        Each test case can include:
        - user_input: The raw user message
        - user_context: Role, settings, and other context passed to the LLM
        - service_catalog: Optional catalog of services for line item matching
        - system_time: Optional ISO timestamp for time-relative queries
        - expected_logic: Expected tool call and/or response substrings
        """
        user_input = case["user_input"]
        expected_logic = case.get("expected_logic", {})
        user_context = case.get("user_context", {})
        service_catalog = case.get("service_catalog")
        system_time = case.get("system_time")
    
        # Extract channel from user_context (defaults to WHATSAPP for backward compat)
        channel_name = user_context.pop("channel", "WHATSAPP") if "channel" in user_context else "WHATSAPP"
    
        parser = LLMParser()
    
        # Execute parsing with all context variables
        result = await parser.parse(
            user_input,
            system_time=system_time,
            service_catalog=service_catalog,
            channel_name=channel_name,
            user_context=user_context
        )
    
        expected_tool = expected_logic.get("tool_called")
        expected_args = expected_logic.get("expected_args", {})
        required_substring = expected_logic.get("required_response_substring")
    
        if expected_tool:
            assert result is not None, f"Expected tool {expected_tool}, but got None"
            actual_tool = result.__class__.__name__
            assert actual_tool == expected_tool, f"Tool mismatch. Expected {expected_tool}, got {actual_tool}"
    
            # Verify arguments
            actual_args = result.dict(exclude_none=True)
            for key, val in expected_args.items():
                assert key in actual_args, f"Missing expected argument '{key}' in {actual_tool}"
    
                # Special handling for floats/rounding
                if isinstance(val, float) and isinstance(actual_args[key], float):
                    assert pytest.approx(actual_args[key]) == val, f"Argument '{key}' mismatch. Expected {val}, got {actual_args[key]}"

                    _verify_line_items(val, actual_args[key])

CREATE TABLE businesses (
	id INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	name VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	payment_link VARCHAR, 
	created_at DATETIME NOT NULL, 
	stripe_customer_id VARCHAR, 
	stripe_subscription_id VARCHAR, 
	subscription_status VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	seat_limit INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	active_addons JSON NOT NULL, 
	quickbooks_connected BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	quickbooks_last_sync DATETIME, 
	clerk_org_id VARCHAR, 
	workflow_invoicing VARCHAR, 
	workflow_quoting VARCHAR, 
	workflow_payment_timing VARCHAR, 
	workflow_tax_inclusive BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_include_payment_terms BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_enable_reminders BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_show_whatsapp_button BOOLEAN, 
	workflow_pipeline_quoted_stage BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_job_creation_default VARCHAR, 
	workflow_distance_unit VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	workflow_auto_quote_followup BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_quote_followup_delay_hrs INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	workflow_auto_review_requests BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	workflow_review_request_delay_hrs INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	workflow_review_link VARCHAR, 
	marketing_settings JSON NOT NULL, 
	default_city VARCHAR, 
	default_country VARCHAR, 
	default_tax_rate FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	invite_code VARCHAR(20), 
	message_count_current_period INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	billing_cycle_anchor DATETIME, 
	message_credits INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	PRIMARY KEY (id), 
	UNIQUE (clerk_org_id)
)
